# Run 20260607T013336Z-66791

- goal source: .dev/goals/252-http-run-concurrency-limit.md
- goal tag:    http-run-concurrency-limit
- provider:    deepseek
- model:       deepseek-chat
- baseline:    359e879

## Goal

```
# Goal 252 — Add concurrency limit to HTTP /run endpoint

**Roadmap**: Arch-review bugfixes (P1 — resource exhaustion)

**Design principle check**:
- Implemented as: `Arc<Semaphore>` in `AppState`, acquired by `/run` and `/sessions/:id/message` handlers
- ❌ Does NOT branch inside `agent.rs::Agent::run`'s main loop

## Why

The HTTP `/run` endpoint (`src/http/handlers.rs`) spins up a fresh
`AgentRuntime` per request with no limit on simultaneous in-flight runs.
Under load this creates N concurrent agent runs, each consuming LLM quota,
shell subprocess capacity, and transcript memory. The rate limiter
(`rate_limit.rs`) caps request rate but not simultaneous in-flight agents.

A `tokio::sync::Semaphore` with a configurable limit is the correct fix.

## Scope (do exactly this, no more)

### 1. `src/config.rs` — add `max_concurrent_runs: usize` to `Config`

Add a field with default `8`:
```rust
/// Maximum number of agent turns running concurrently in HTTP mode.
/// 0 means unlimited (not recommended for production).
#[serde(default = "default_max_concurrent_runs")]
pub max_concurrent_runs: usize,
```

Add the default function:
```rust
fn default_max_concurrent_runs() -> usize { 8 }
```

### 2. `src/http/mod.rs` — add semaphore to `AppState`

Add a field to `AppState`:
```rust
/// Limits simultaneous in-flight agent runs.
pub run_semaphore: Arc<tokio::sync::Semaphore>,
```

In the `AppState` construction site (wherever `AppState { ... }` is built,
likely in `src/main.rs` or `src/http/mod.rs`), initialize it:
```rust
run_semaphore: Arc::new(tokio::sync::Semaphore::new(config.max_concurrent_runs.max(1))),
```

### 3. `src/http/handlers.rs` — acquire semaphore permit in `run_handler` and `session_message_handler`

In the `run_handler` function (the `POST /run` handler), acquire a permit
before creating the `AgentRuntime`:

```rust
let _permit = state
    .run_semaphore
    .acquire()
    .await
    .map_err(|_| (StatusCode::SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE, Json(json!({
        "error": "server shutting down"
    }))))?;
```

Do the same in `session_message_handler` (the `POST /sessions/:id/message`
handler), since that also runs an agent turn.

The `_permit` is dropped at end of handler scope, releasing the slot.

If `max_concurrent_runs` is 0, the semaphore with `max(1)` still works
(minimum 1). If you want to support "unlimited", use
`tokio::sync::Semaphore::MAX_PERMITS` when value is 0:
```rust
let permits = if config.max_concurrent_runs == 0 {
    tokio::sync::Semaphore::MAX_PERMITS
} else {
    config.max_concurrent_runs
};
run_semaphore: Arc::new(tokio::sync::Semaphore::new(permits)),
```

### 4. Tests

Add one unit test or integration test verifying that with `max_concurrent_runs = 1`,
a second concurrent `/run` request blocks until the first completes. Keep it
simple — a mock or a direct semaphore test is fine.

## Acceptance

- `cargo test --workspace` green
- `cargo clippy --all-targets --all-features -- -D warnings` clean
- `cargo fmt --all` clean
- `Config` has `max_concurrent_runs` field with default 8
- `AppState` has `run_semaphore: Arc<Semaphore>`
- Both `run_handler` and `session_message_handler` acquire the semaphore before
  launching an agent turn

## Notes for the agent

- Read `src/config.rs` to understand Config struct pattern (serde defaults).
- Read `src/http/mod.rs` to see `AppState` and where it is constructed.
- Read `src/http/handlers.rs` to find `run_handler` and `session_message_handler`.
- Grep for `AppState {` to find all construction sites.
- Do NOT touch `src/agent.rs`, `src/runtime.rs`, `src/kernel.rs`, or any LLM provider.
- `tokio::sync::Semaphore` is already a dependency (tokio full features are used).
- Run `cargo test --workspace` before declaring done.
- **DO NOT call `exit_plan_mode` or `request_plan_mode`.** Running headless.
```

        tool_calls: None,

Sensible\n//! defaults make the binary runnable with just `RECURSIVE_API_KEY` and\n//! `RECURSIVE_MODEL` set.\n\nuse std::path::{Path, PathBuf};\n\nuse crate::error::{Error, Result};\nuse crate::providers::{find_preset, ProviderPreset};\nuse crate::tools::episodic_recall::episodic_recall_summary;\nuse crate::tools::facts::facts_summary;\nuse crate::tools::memory::memory_summary;\nuse crate::tools::memory::scratchpad_summary;\n\n#[derive(Clone)]\npub struct Config {\n    pub workspace: PathBuf,\n    pub api_base: String,\n    pub api_key: Option<String>,\n    pub model: String,\n    pub provider_type: String,\n    /// Preset id resolved from `provider.preset` in the config file.\n    /// `None` when the user did not opt in (or the file was absent).\n    pub preset: Option<String>,\n    pub max_steps: usize,\n    pub temperature: f64,\n    pub system_prompt: String,\n    pub retry_max: usize,\n    pub retry_initial_backoff_secs: u64,\n    pub retry_max_backoff_secs: u64,\n    pub shell_timeout_secs: u64,\n    /// Run in headless mode: interactive tools go through external hooks\n    /// instead of waiting for terminal input. If no hook approves the call,\n    /// the tool is auto-denied.\n    pub headless: bool,\n    pub memory_summary_limit: usize,\n    /// Extended thinking budget for models that support it (e.g. Anthropic claude-3-7).\n    /// `None` = model default; `Some(0)` = disable thinking; `Some(n)` = budget_tokens.\n    pub thinking_budget: Option<u32>,\n    /// Optional display name for the session, shown in the /resume picker.\n    pub session_name: Option<String>,\n    /// Maximum total API spend in USD for this run. Checked after each turn.\n    /// `None` = no limit.\n    pub max_budget_usd: Option<f64>,\n    /// Additional workspace-root directories the agent is allowed to access\n    /// (sandbox expansion via `--add-dir`). Empty = only `workspace`.\n    pub extra_dirs: Vec<std::path::PathBuf>,\n    /// If non-empty, only tools whose names appear in this list are registered.\n    /// Set via `--allow-tools` CLI flag or `RECURSIVE_ALLOW_TOOLS` env var.\n    pub allow_tools: Vec<String>,\n    /// Override the detected context window size for the configured model.\n    /// When set, `context_window_tokens()` returns this value instead of the\n    /// value from providers.toml. Useful for custom deployments where the\n    /// actual context window differs from the preset default.\n    pub context_window_override: Option<usize>,\n    /// Maximum nesting depth for sub-agents and parallel workers.\n    /// Read from `RECURSIVE_SUBAGENT_MAX_DEPTH` env var, defaults to 2.\n    pub subagent_max_depth: usize,\n    /// When `false` (default), API callers who request `\"bypass\"` permission\n    /// mode are silently downgraded to `Default`. Set to `true` via\n    /// `RECURSIVE_ALLOW_BYPASS_PERMISSIONS=1` to honour bypass requests.\n    pub allow_bypass_permissions: bool,\n    /// Maximum number of ToolSearchTool round-trips per\n    /// `complete_with_search` / `stream_with_search` call.\n    /// Defaults to 3. Set via `RECURSIVE_MAX_SEARCH_ROUNDS`.\n    pub max_search_rounds: usize,\n    /// Number of recent steps to check for stuck detection. Default 10.\n    /// Set via `RECURSIVE_STUCK_WINDOW`.\n    pub stuck_window: usize,\n    /// Fraction of steps in the window that must be errors to declare \"stuck\".\n    /// Default 0.8. Set via `RECURSIVE_STUCK_ERROR_RATE`.\n    pub stuck_error_rate: f64,\n    /// Maximum number of concurrent agent runs across all HTTP endpoints.\n    /// `0` means unlimited. Defaults to 8.\n    /// Set via `RECURSIVE_MAX_CONCURRENT_RUNS` env var.\n    pub max_concurrent_runs: usize,\n}\n\nimpl std::fmt::Debug for Config {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {\n        f.debug_struct(\"Config\")\n            .field(\"workspace\", &self.workspace)\n            .field(\"api_base\", &self.api_base)\n            .field(\"api_key\", &self.api_key.as_ref().map(|_| \"[REDACTED]\"))\n            .field(\"model\", &self.model)\n            .field(\"provider_type\", &self.provider_type)\n            .field(\"preset\", &self.preset)\n            .field(\"max_steps\", &self.max_steps)\n            .field(\"temperature\", &self.temperature)\n            .field(\"system_prompt\", &self.system_prompt)\n            .field(\"retry_max\", &self.retry_max)\n            .field(\n                \"retry_initial_backoff_secs\",\n                &self.retry_initial_backoff_secs,\n &self.session_name)\n            .field(\"max_budget_usd\", &self.max_budget_usd)\n            .field(\"extra_dirs\", &self.extra_dirs)\n            .field(\"allow_tools\", &self.allow_tools)\n            .field(\"context_window_override\", &self.context_window_override)\n            .field(\"subagent_max_depth\", &self.subagent_max_depth)\n            .field(\"allow_bypass_permissions\", &self.allow_bypass_permissions)\n            .field(\"max_search_rounds\", &self.max_search_rounds)\n            .field(\"stuck_window\", &self.stuck_window)\n            .field(\"stuck_error_rate\", &self.stuck_error_rate)\n            .field(\"max_concurrent_runs\", &self.max_concurrent_runs)\n            .finish()\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Config {\n    /// Return the effective context window size for the configured model.\n    ///\n    /// Prefers `context_window_override` when set; otherwise falls back to the\n    /// value from the bundled `providers.toml` via `context_window_tokens_for_model`.\n    pub fn context_window_tokens(&self) -> usize {\n        self.context_window_override\n            .unwrap_or_else(|| crate::llm::context_window_tokens_for_model(&self.model))\n    }\n\n    /// Load from environment, with config file (~/.recursive/config.toml) as fallback.\n    ///\n    /// Precedence (highest first), applied to `api_base` / `api_key` / `model` /\n    /// `provider_type`:\n    ///\n    ///   1. env var (e.g. `RECURSIVE_API_BASE`, `OPENAI_API_KEY`)\n    ///   2. explicit field in the file's `[provider]` section\n    ///   3. preset field — `provider.preset = \"<id>\"` looks up the bundled\n    ///      `providers.toml` and takes its `api_base` / `default_model` /\n    ///      `provider_type`. For `api_key`, step 3 instead consults\n    ///      `std::env::var(preset.key_env)` (e.g. `DEEPSEEK_API_KEY`).\n    ///   4. hardcoded default\n    ///\n    /// The api_key chain is asymmetric: the *generic* env vars in step 1\n    /// (`RECURSIVE_API_KEY` / `OPENAI_API_KEY`) rank above the file's explicit\n    /// `api_key`, but a preset's *specific* env var in step 3 ranks below it.\n    /// Inverting step 3 would silently override a user's `api_key = \"sk-old\"`\n    /// whenever `DEEPSEEK_API_KEY` happened to be in their shell.\n    ///\n    /// The API key is optional here so commands that don't need the LLM\n    /// (e.g. `tools`, `config`) still run.\n    pub fn from_env() -> Result<Self> {\n        // Load file config (lowest priority, used as fallback)\n        let file_config = crate::config_file::FileConfig::load()\n            .map_err(|e| Error::Config {\n                message: format!(\"config file: {e}\"),\n            })?\n            .unwrap_or_default();\n        let file_provider = file_config.provider.as_ref();\n        let file_agent = file_config.agent.as_ref();\n\n        // Resolve preset (if any). Unknown id is a hard error so users\n        // see a typo at startup rather than silent default-fallback.\n        let preset: Option<&'static ProviderPreset> =\n            match file_provider.and_then(|p| p.preset.as_deref()) {\n                None => None,\n                Some(id) => Some(find_preset(id).ok_or_else(|| {\n                    let known: Vec<&str> = crate::providers::all_presets()\n                        .iter()\n                        .map(|p| p.id.as_str())\n                        .collect();\n                    Error::Config {\n                        message: format!(\n                            \"provider.preset = {:?} not found in providers.toml. Valid ids: {}\",\n                            id,\n                            known.join(\", \"),\n                        ),\n                    }\n                })?),\n            };\n\n        let workspace = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_WORKSPACE\")\n            .map(PathBuf::from)\n            .unwrap_or_else(|_| std::env::current_dir().unwrap_or_else(|_| PathBuf::from(\".\")));\n\n        // provider_type must be resolved before api_base so we can pick the\n        // correct endpoint for dual-protocol presets (e.g. DeepSeek supports\n        // both OpenAI-compatible /v1 and Anthropic Messages API endpoints).\n        let provider_type = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_PROVIDER_TYPE\")\n            .ok()\n            .or_else(|| file_provider.and_then(|p| p.provider_type.clone()))\n            .or_else(|| preset.map(|p| p.provider_type.clone()))\n            .unwrap_or_else(|| \"anthropic\".into());\n\n        // When the user requests the Anthropic protocol and the preset has a\n        // dedicated Anthropic endpoint, prefer that over the default api_base.\n        let preset_api_base = preset.map(|p| {\n            if provider_type == \"anthropic\" {\n                p.anthropic_api_base\n                    .as_deref()\n                    .unwrap_or(&p.api_base)\n                    .to_string()\n            } else {\n                p.api_base.clone()\n            }\n        });\n\n        let api_base = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_API_BASE\")\n            .or_else(|_| std::env::var(\"OPENAI_API_BASE\"))\n            .ok()\n            .or_else(|| file_provider.and_then(|p| p.api_base.clone()))\n            .or(preset_api_base)\n            .unwrap_or_else(|| \"https://api.anthropic.com\".into());\n\n        // api_key chain: generic env (above file) → file explicit → preset's\n        // key_env (below file, so explicit file wins) → None.\n        let api_key = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_API_KEY\")\n            .or_else(|_| std::env::var(\"OPENAI_API_KEY\"))\n            .ok()\n            .or_else(|| file_provider.and_then(|p| p.api_key.clone()))\n            .or_else(|| {\n                preset\n                    .filter(|p| !p.key_env.is_empty())\n                    .and_then(|p| std::env::var(&p.key_env).ok())\n            });\n\n        let model = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_MODEL\")\n            .or_else(|_| std::env::var(\"OPENAI_MODEL\"))\n            .ok()\n            .or_else(|| file_provider.and_then(|p| p.model.clone()))\n            .or_else(|| preset.map(|p| p.default_model.clone()))\n            .unwrap_or_else(|| \"claude-sonnet-4-6\".into());\n\n        let max_steps = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_MAX_STEPS\")\n            .ok()\n            .and_then(|s| s.parse().ok())\n            .or_else(|| file_agent.and_then(|a| a.max_steps))\n            .unwrap_or(32);\n\n        let temperature = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_TEMPERATURE\")\n            .ok()\n            .and_then(|s| s.parse().ok())\n            .or_else(|| file_agent.and_then(|a| a.temperature))\n            .unwrap_or(0.2);\n\n        let system_prompt = match std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_SYSTEM_PROMPT_FILE\") {\n            Ok(path) => std::fs::read_to_string(&path).map_err(|e| Error::Config {\n                message: format!(\"read system prompt {path}: {e}\"),\n            })?,\n            Err(_) => default_system_prompt(),\n        };\n\n        let retry_max = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_RETRY_MAX\")\n            .ok()\n            .and_then(|s| s.parse().ok())\n            .unwrap_or(2);\n        let retry_initial_backoff_secs = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_RETRY_INITIAL_BACKOFF_SECS\")\n            .ok()\n            .and_then(|s| s.parse().ok())\n            .unwrap_or(1);\n        let retry_max_backoff_secs = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_RETRY_MAX_BACKOFF_SECS\")\n            .ok()\n            .and_then(|s| s.parse().ok())\n            .unwrap_or(8);\n        let shell_timeout_secs = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_SHELL_TIMEOUT_SECS\")\n            .ok()\n            .and_then(|s| s.parse().ok())\n            .or_else(|| file_agent.and_then(|a| a.shell_timeout_secs))\n            .unwrap_or(300);\n\n        let headless = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_HEADLESS\")\n            .ok()\n            .map(|s| s == \"1\" || s.eq_ignore_ascii_case(\"true\"))\n            .unwrap_or(false);\n\n        let memory_summary_limit = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_MEMORY_SUMMARY_LIMIT\")\n            .ok()\n            .and_then(|s| s.parse().ok())\n            .unwrap_or(5);\n\n        let subagent_max_depth = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_SUBAGENT_MAX_DEPTH\")\n            .ok()\n            .and_then(|s| s.parse().ok())\n            .unwrap_or(2);\n\n        let allow_bypass_permissions = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_ALLOW_BYPASS_PERMISSIONS\")\n            .ok()\n            .map(|s| s == \"1\" || s.eq_ignore_ascii_case(\"true\"))\n            .unwrap_or(false);\n\n        let max_search_rounds = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_MAX_SEARCH_ROUNDS\")\n            .ok()\n            .and_then(|s| s.parse().ok())\n            .unwrap_or(3);\n\n        let stuck_window = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_STUCK_WINDOW\")\n            .ok()\n            .and_then(|s| s.parse().ok())\n            .unwrap_or(10usize);\n\n        let stuck_error_rate = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_STUCK_ERROR_RATE\")\n            .ok()\n            .and_then(|s| s.parse().ok())\n            .unwrap_or(0.8f64);\n\n        let max_concurrent_runs = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_MAX_CONCURRENT_RUNS\")\n            .ok()\n            .and_then(|s| s.parse().ok())\n            .unwrap_or(8usize);\n\n        // Assemble system prompt with memory layers.\n        // Order: most stable first (user.md), most volatile last (memory_summary).\n        // This helps LLM prefix caching.\n        let mut layers: Vec<(String, String)> = Vec::new();\n\n        // Layer 1: User preferences (global, ~/.recursive/memory/user.md)\n        if let Some(user_memory) = load_user_memory() {\n            layers.push((\"# User preferences\".into(), user_memory));\n        }\n\n        // Layer 2: Project memory (workspace-local, agent-writable)\n        if let Some(project_memory) = load_project_memory(&workspace) {\n            layers.push((\"# Project memory\".into(), project_memory));\n        }\n\n        // Layer 3: Memory summary (volatile, changes each run)\n        let memory_block = memory_summary(&workspace, memory_summary_limit);\n        if !memory_block.is_empty() {\n            layers.push((\"# Memory summary\".into(), memory_block));\n        }\n\n        // Layer 4: Scratchpad summary\n        let scratchpad_block = scratchpad_summary(&workspace);\n        if !scratchpad_block.is_empty() {\n            layers.push((\"# Scratchpad\".into(), scratchpad_block));\n        }\n\n        // Layer 5: Facts summary\n        let facts_block = facts_summary(&workspace, memory_summary_limit);\n        if !facts_block.is_empty() {\n            layers.push((\"# Facts\".into(), facts_block));\n        }\n\n        // Layer 6: Episodic recall summary\n        let episodic_block = episodic_recall_summary(&workspace, memory_summary_limit);\n        if !episodic_block.is_empty() {\n            layers.push((\"# Episodic recall\".into(), episodic_block));\n        }\n\n        // Build the final system prompt: base prompt + layers\n        let system_prompt = if layers.is_empty() {\n            system_prompt\n        } else {\n            let mut result = system_prompt;\n            result.push_str(\"\\n\\n---\\n\\n\");\n            for (i, (heading, content)) in layers.iter().enumerate() {\n                if i > 0 {\n                    result.push_str(\"\\n\\n\");\n                }\n                result.push_str(heading);\n                result.push('\\n');\n                result.push_str(content);\n            }\n            result\n        };\n\n        Ok(Self {\n            workspace,\n            api_base,\n            api_key,\n            model,\n            provider_type,\n            preset: preset.map(|p| p.id.clone()),\n            max_steps,\n            temperature,\n            system_prompt,\n            retry_max,\n            retry_initial_backoff_secs,\n            retry_max_backoff_secs,\n            shell_timeout_secs,\n            headless,\n            memory_summary_limit,\n            thinking_budget: None,\n            session_name: None,\n            max_budget_usd: None,\n            extra_dirs: Vec::new(),\n            allow_tools: Vec::new(),\n            context_window_override: None,\n            subagent_max_depth,\n            allow_bypass_permissions,\n            max_search_rounds,\n            stuck_window,\n            stuck_error_rate,\n            max_concurrent_runs,\n        })\n    }\n\n    /// Return the API key or a descriptive error if none was configured.\n    pub fn require_api_key(&self) -> Result<&str> {\n        self.api_key.as_deref().ok_or_else(|| Error::Config {\n            message: \"set RECURSIVE_API_KEY (or OPENAI_API_KEY), or set RECURSIVE_PROVIDER_TYPE and the matching provider's *_API_KEY env var\".into(),\n        })\n    }\n\n    /// Validate that the config has enough information to run the agent.\n    /// Returns a user-friendly error message if not.\n    pub fn validate_for_agent(&self) -> std::result::Result<(), String> {\n        if self.api_key.is_none() || self.api_key.as_deref() == Some(\"\") {\n            return Err(\"\\\nError: No API key configured.\n\nSet one of:\n  --api-key <KEY>\n  RECURSIVE_API_KEY=<KEY>\n  OPENAI_API_KEY=<KEY>\n\nOr use a preset (auto-fills api_base / model / type, pulls the key from\nthe preset's env var like DEEPSEEK_API_KEY):\n  recursive init --provider deepseek\n  # or write ~/.recursive/config.toml:\n  [provider]\n  preset = \\\"deepseek\\\"\n\nExample:\n  recursive --api-key sk-xxx --model deepseek-chat run \\\"hello\\\"\n\"\n            .to_string());\n        }\n        if ![\"openai\", \"anthropic\"].contains(&self.provider_type.as_str()) {\n            return Err(format!(\n                \"\\\nError: Unknown provider type '{}'.\n\nSupported providers: openai, anthropic\nSet via --provider, RECURSIVE_PROVIDER_TYPE, or by using\n`provider.preset = \\\"<id>\\\"` in ~/.recursive/config.toml.\n\",\n                self.provider_type\n            ));\n        }\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\npub fn default_system_prompt() -> String {\n    [\n        \"You are Recursive, a minimal but capable coding agent.\",\n        \"\",\n        \"Tools available: Read, Write, Edit, Bash, Grep, Glob.\",\n        \"Additional tools: estimate_tokens (estimate token count for text or file).\",\n        \"All file paths are workspace-relative; the sandbox will reject anything outside.\",\n        \"\",\n        \"Working principles:\",\n        \"- Read before you write. Skim relevant files (Read, Glob, Grep) before editing.\",\n        \"- Prefer Edit over Write when modifying existing files. Use Write only for new files or full rewrites.\",\n        \"- After any non-trivial code change, run the project's tests via Bash and quote the result.\",\n        \"- If a tool call fails the same way twice, change approach instead of retrying.\",\n        \"- Stop calling tools and write a short final summary once the task is done.\",\n        \"\",\n        \"Don't:\",\n        \"- Do not run `git checkout`, `git reset`, `git restore`, or any command that mutates the working tree. The orchestrator owns rollback.\",\n        \"- Do not edit source files via `sed -i`, `tail > file`, or `cat <<EOF`. Use Edit or Write (whole file).\",\n        \"- Verify behavior via `cargo test`, never via `cargo run | jq`. Cargo build noise on a fresh tree breaks jq parsing and burns your step budget.\",\n        \"\",\n        \"Output should be terse and concrete. Avoid filler.\",\n        \"\",\n        \"## Task List Management\",\n        \"\",\n        \"Use TodoWrite to track progress on complex tasks with 3 or more distinct steps.\",\n        \"\",\n        \"When to use:\",\n        \"- Create the list BEFORE starting work (capture requirements as todos)\",\n        \"- Update status in real-time as you work\",\n        \"- Mark exactly ONE task as in_progress at a time\",\n        \"- Mark completed IMMEDIATELY after finishing (not batched)\",\n        \"- ONLY mark completed when fully done (tests passing, no partial work)\",\n        \"- Clear the list (call with empty array) when all tasks are done\",\n        \"\",\n        \"When NOT to use:\",\n        \"- Single, straightforward tasks\",\n        \"- Purely conversational responses\",\n        \"- Tasks completable in less than 3 trivial steps\",\n        \"\",\n        \"## Planning Mode\",\n        \"\",\n        \"Use enter_plan_mode when:\",\n        \"- The task requires exploring 3+ files before deciding what to change\",\n        \"- The task touches architectural boundaries (new module, new tool, API change)\",\n        \"- You are unsure of the correct approach and want to discuss options first\",\n        \"\",\n        \"While in plan mode:\",\n        \"- Read files freely (Read, Glob, Grep)\",\n        \"- Think through trade-offs in your responses\",\n        \"- DO NOT call Write, Edit, or Bash\",\n        \"- When you have a clear plan, call exit_plan_mode with a markdown summary\",\n        \"\",\n        \"Your plan should include:\",\n        \"1. What you understand about the current code\",\n        \"2. The approach you propose and why\",\n        \"3. Files you will modify and how\",\n        \"4. How you will verify the change is correct\",\n    ]\n    .join(\"\\n\")\n}\n\n/// Maximum size for project context file (AGENTS.md) in bytes.\n/// 16 KB is enough for a detailed project context without blowing\n/// the context window.\nconst MAX_PROJECT_CONTEXT_SIZE: usize = 16 * 1024;\n\n/// Maximum size for memory files (user.md, project.md) in bytes.\nconst MAX_MEMORY_FILE_SIZE: usize = 8 * 1024;\n\n/// Load user-global memory from ~/.recursive/memory/user.md.\n/// Returns None if the file doesn't exist. Caps at 8KB.\npub fn load_user_memory() -> Option<String> {\n    let home = std::env::var(\"HOME\").ok()?;\n    let path = PathBuf::from(home).join(\".recursive/memory/user.md\");\n    load_memory_file(&path)\n}\n\n/// Load project-local memory (agent-writable) from workspace/.recursive/memory/project.md.\npub fn load_project_memory(workspace: &Path) -> Option<String> {\n    let path = workspace.join(\".recursive/memory/project.md\");\n    load_memory_file(&path)\n}\n\n/// Load a memory file with an 8KB cap.\nfn load_memory_file(path: &Path) -> Option<String> {\n    if !path.is_file() {\n        return None;\n    }\n    let content = std::fs::read_to_string(path).ok()?;\n    if content.is_empty() {\n        return None;\n    }\n    if content.len() > MAX_MEMORY_FILE_SIZE {\n        Some(format!(\n            \"{}\\n\\n[…truncated at 8KB]\",\n            &content[..MAX_MEMORY_FILE_SIZE]\n        ))\n    } else {\n        Some(content)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Load project context from AGENTS.md at workspace root.\n///\n/// Returns the file content if present, truncated to 16 KB with a\n/// marker if larger. Returns None if absent.\npub fn load_project_context(workspace: &Path) -> Option<String> {\n    let path = workspace.join(\"AGENTS.md\");\n    if !path.exists() {\n        return None;\n    }\n\n    let metadata = std::fs::metadata(&path).ok()?;\n    let file_size = metadata.len() as usize;\n\n    if file_size <= MAX_PROJECT_CONTEXT_SIZE {\n        let content = std::fs::read_to_string(&path).ok()?;\n        Some(content)\n    } else {\n        // File is too large: read first 16 KB and append truncation marker\n        let mut file = std::fs::File::open(&path).ok()?;\n        use std::io::Read;\n        let mut buffer = vec![0u8; MAX_PROJECT_CONTEXT_SIZE];\n        let bytes_read = file.read(&mut buffer).ok()?;\n        buffer.truncate(bytes_read);\n        let content = String::from_utf8_lossy(&buffer).to_string();\n        let truncated_msg = format!(\n            \"\\n\\n[…truncated, AGENTS.md is {} KB; consider trimming for fresh agent sessions]\",\n            file_size / 1024\n        );\n        Some(content + &truncated_msg)\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    #[test]\n    fn default_prompt_is_well_under_a_kilobyte() {\n        // Goal-167 added a task-list section; Goal-165 added Planning Mode.\n        // Bump the limit to 6 KiB to accommodate both additions.\n        assert!(default_system_prompt().len() < 6144);\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn default_prompt_mentions_bash_tests() {\n        let prompt = default_system_prompt();\n        assert!(prompt.contains(\"Bash\"));\n        assert!(prompt.contains(\"tests\"));\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn default_prompt_includes_new_sections() {\n        let prompt = default_system_prompt();\n        assert!(prompt.contains(\"Edit\"));\n        assert!(prompt.contains(\"git checkout\"));\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn retry_defaults_match_old_policy() {\n        // Ensure defaults match the hardcoded RetryPolicy::default()\n        let config = Config {\n            workspace: PathBuf::from(\".\"),\n            api_base: String::new(),\n            api_key: None,\n            model: String::new(),\n            provider_type: \"openai\".into(),\n            preset: None,\n            max_steps: 32,\n            temperature: 0.2,\n            system_prompt: String::new(),\n            retry_max: 2,\n            retry_initial_backoff_secs: 1,\n            retry_max_backoff_secs: 8,\n            shell_timeout_secs: 300,\n            headless: false,\n            memory_summary_limit: 5,\n            thinking_budget: None,\n            session_name: None,\n            max_budget_usd: None,\n            extra_dirs: Vec::new(),\n            allow_tools: Vec::new(),\n            context_window_override: None,\n            subagent_max_depth: 2,\n            allow_bypass_permissions: false,\n            max_search_rounds: 3,\n            stuck_window: 10,\n            stuck_error_rate: 0.8,\n            max_concurrent_runs: 8,\n        };\n        assert_eq!(config.retry_max, 2);\n        assert_eq!(config.retry_initial_backoff_secs, 1);\n        assert_eq!(config.retry_max_backoff_secs, 8);\n        assert_eq!(config.shell_timeout_secs, 300);\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn retry_env_overrides_apply() {\n        // Hold the env lock — this test mutates RECURSIVE_RETRY_*, RECURSIVE_MODEL,\n        // RECURSIVE_API_KEY, which race with provider_preset_resolution_chain and\n        // similar tests without the lock.\n        let _env_lock = crate::test_util::env_lock();\n        // Save original env values\n        let original_max = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_RETRY_MAX\");\n        let original_initial = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_RETRY_INITIAL_BACKOFF_SECS\");\n        let original_max_backoff = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_RETRY_MAX_BACKOFF_SECS\");\n\n        // Set custom values\n        std::env::set_var(\"RECURSIVE_RETRY_MAX\", \"5\");\n        std::env::set_var(\"RECURSIVE_RETRY_INITIAL_BACKOFF_SECS\", \"2\");\n        std::env::set_var(\"RECURSIVE_RETRY_MAX_BACKOFF_SECS\", \"30\");\n\n        // We need to also set required env vars to avoid errors\n        std::env::set_var(\"RECURSIVE_MODEL\", \"test-model\");\n        std::env::set_var(\"RECURSIVE_API_KEY\", \"test-key\");\n\n        let config = Config::from_env().unwrap();\n\n        assert_eq!(config.retry_max, 5);\n        assert_eq!(config.retry_initial_backoff_secs, 2);\n        assert_eq!(config.retry_max_backoff_secs, 30);\n\n        // Restore original env values\n        std::env::remove_var(\"RECURSIVE_RETRY_MAX\");\n        std::env::remove_var(\"RECURSIVE_RETRY_INITIAL_BACKOFF_SECS\");\n        std::env::remove_var(\"RECURSIVE_RETRY_MAX_BACKOFF_SECS\");\n        std::env::remove_var(\"RECURSIVE_MODEL\");\n        std::env::remove_var(\"RECURSIVE_API_KEY\");\n\n        if let Ok(v) = original_max {\n            std::env::set_var(\"RECURSIVE_RETRY_MAX\", v);\n        }\n        if let Ok(v) = original_initial {\n            std::env::set_var(\"RECURSIVE_RETRY_INITIAL_BACKOFF_SECS\", v);\n        }\n        if let Ok(v) = original_max_backoff {\n            std::env::set_var(\"RECURSIVE_RETRY_MAX_BACKOFF_SECS\", v);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // NOTE: both shell_timeout_* checks live in ONE test on purpose.\n    // `cargo test` runs tests in parallel threads and `set_var` /\n    // `remove_var` are process-global, so splitting them creates a\n    // race (one test sees the other's value). MiniMax's goal-23 run\n    // burned 50 steps discovering this exact race; lesson recorded in\n    // AGENTS.md section 5.\n    #[test]\n    fn shell_timeout_default_and_env_override() {\n        // This test mutates RECURSIVE_MODEL / RECURSIVE_API_KEY /\n        // RECURSIVE_SHELL_TIMEOUT_SECS — hold the env lock so we don't race\n        // with other tests that read or write the same vars.\n        let _env_lock = crate::test_util::env_lock();\n        let original = std::env::var(\"RECURSIVE_SHELL_TIMEOUT_SECS\").ok();\n        std::env::set_var(\"RECURSIVE_MODEL\", \"test-model\");\n        std::env::set_var(\"RECURSIVE_API_KEY\", \"test-key\");\n\n        std::env::remove_var(\"RECURSIVE_SHELL_TIMEOUT_SECS\");\n        let config = Config::from_env().unwrap();\n        assert_eq!(config.shell_timeout_secs, 300);\n\n        std::env::set_var(\"RECURSIVE_SHELL_TIMEOUT_SECS\", \"42\");\n        let config = Config::from_env().unwrap();\n        assert_eq!(config.shell_timeout_secs, 42);\n\n        if let Some(v) = original {\n            std::env::set_var(\"RECURSIVE_SHELL_TIMEOUT_SECS\", v);\n        } else {\n            std::env::remove_var(\"RECURSIVE_SHELL_TIMEOUT_SECS\");\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Tests for load_project_context\n    #[test]\n    fn test_a_load_project_context_with_small_file() {\n        let tmp = tempfile::tempdir().expect(\"tempdir\");\n        let path = tmp.path().join(\"AGENTS.md\");\n        std::fs::write(&path, \"# Project Context\\n\\nHello world\").expect(\"write\");\n\n        let content = load_project_context(tmp.path());\n        assert!(content.is_some());\n        assert!(content.unwrap().contains(\"Hello world\"));\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_b_load_project_context_truncates_large_file() {\n        let tmp = tempfile::tempdir().expect(\"tempdir\");\n        let path = tmp.path().join(\"AGENTS.md\");\n        // Write 20 KB of content\n        let large_content = \"x\".repeat(20 * 1024);\n        std::fs::write(&path, large_content).expect(\"write\");\n\n        let content = load_project_context(tmp.path());\n        assert!(content.is_some());\n        let c = content.unwrap();\n        // Should contain truncation marker\n        assert!(c.contains(\"truncated\"));\n        assert!(c.contains(\"20 KB\"));\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_c_load_project_context_none_when_missing() {\n        let tmp = tempfile::tempdir().expect(\"tempdir\");\n        // No AGENTS.md file\n        let content = load_project_context(tmp.path());\n        assert!(content.is_none());\n    }\n\n    // --- Memory layer tests ---\n    //\n    // NOTE: Tests that set HOME are consolidated into ONE test to avoid\n    // races with parallel test execution (set_var is process-global).\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_b_load_project_memory_returns_content() {\n        let tmp = tempfile::tempdir().expect(\"tempdir\");\n\n        let mem_dir = tmp.path().join(\".recursive/memory\");\n        std::fs::create_dir_all(&mem_dir).expect(\"create dirs\");\n        let path = mem_dir.join(\"project.md\");\n        std::fs::write(&path, \"This project uses AGPL license\").expect(\"write\");\n\n        let content = load_project_memory(tmp.path());\n        assert!(content.is_some());\n        assert!(content.unwrap().contains(\"AGPL\"));\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_c_files_exceeding_8kb_are_truncated() {\n        let tmp = tempfile::tempdir().expect(\"tempdir\");\n\n        let mem_dir = tmp.path().join(\".recursive/memory\");\n        std::fs::create_dir_all(&mem_dir).expect(\"create dirs\");\n        let path = mem_dir.join(\"project.md\");\n        // Write 10 KB of content\n        let large_content = \"Hello world\\n\".repeat(800);\n        assert!(large_content.len() > 8192, \"content must exceed 8KB\");\n        std::fs::write(&path, &large_content).expect(\"write\");\n\n        let content = load_project_memory(tmp.path());\n        assert!(content.is_some());\n        let c = content.unwrap();\n        // Should contain truncation marker\n        assert!(c.contains(\"truncated at 8KB\"));\n        // Should not contain the full content\n        assert!(c.len() < large_content.len());\n    }\n\n    // Consolidated test for all HOME-dependent memory checks.\n    // These must be ONE test because set_var(\"HOME\", ...) is process-global\n    // and parallel tests would race on it. The PinnedHome guard holds the\n    // cross-module env lock for the whole body, so other tests that read\n    // HOME (e.g. facts, migrate, paths) cannot observe a torn-down state.\n    #[test]\n protected by PinnedRecursiveHome (which only pins RECURSIVE_HOME).\n        // Holding env_lock here serialises us with all other tests that\n        // use PinnedHome / PinnedRecursiveHome / env_lock HOME.get_or_init(|| tempfile::tempdir().expect(\"tempdir\"));\n        let _g = crate::test_util::PinnedRecursiveHomeNoLock::new(tmp.path(), &_env_lock);\n        let config_path = and\n/// POST /sessions/:id/messages, both of which accept unbounded user strings.\nconst MAX_BODY_BYTES: usize = 1024 * 1024;\nuse std::collections::HashMap;\nuse std::sync::atomic::AtomicU64;\nuse std::sync::Arc;\nuse tokio::sync::{broadcast, RwLock};\n\nuse crate::config::Config;\nuse crate::llm::LlmProvider;\nuse crate::runtime::AgentRuntime;\nuse crate::tools::plan_mode::PlanApprovalGate;\nuse crate::tools::ToolRegistry;\n\n// ── Metrics ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Prometheus-compatible metrics collector using lock-free atomic counters.\n#[derive(Default)]\npub struct Metrics {\n    pub requests_total: AtomicU64,\n    pub requests_active: AtomicU64,\n    pub agent_runs_total: AtomicU64,\n    pub agent_runs_success: AtomicU64,\n    pub agent_runs_failed: AtomicU64,\n    pub tokens_prompt_total: AtomicU64,\n    pub tokens_completion_total: AtomicU64,\n    pub agent_steps_total: AtomicU64,\n}\n\n// ── Session types ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Internal session state (not directly serialized to clients).\n///\n/// The [`AgentRuntime`] owns the transcript; this struct adds HTTP-layer\n/// metadata (id, created_at) and the broadcast channel for SSE clients.\npub struct SessionState {\n    pub id: String,\n    pub created_at: String,\n    /// Optional human-readable title, settable via `PATCH /sessions/:id`.\n    pub title: Option<String>,\n    /// Runtime is wrapped in a per-session Mutex so concurrent HTTP requests\n    /// for the same session are serialized without blocking the global lock.\n    pub runtime: Arc<tokio::sync::Mutex<AgentRuntime>>,\n    /// Shared gate for plan-mode approval. Stored here so HTTP handlers can\n    /// approve/reject without taking the runtime Mutex (which may be held\n    /// by a running agent turn).\n    pub plan_approval_gate: Arc<PlanApprovalGate>,\n    /// Goal-170: cancellation token for the currently running agent turn.\n    /// `POST /sessions/:id/interrupt` cancels this token, which causes\n    /// the kernel to exit with `FinishReason::Cancelled` at the next step\n    /// boundary.  Replaced with a fresh token at the start of every turn.\n    pub interrupt_token: Arc<tokio::sync::Mutex<Option<tokio_util::sync::CancellationToken>>>,\n    /// Approximate non-system message count, updated atomically as messages\n    /// are appended. Allows `list_sessions` to read the count without taking\n    /// the runtime Mutex (which may be held by a running agent turn).\n    pub non_system_message_count: Arc<std::sync::atomic::AtomicUsize>,\n    pub last_active: Arc<std::sync::Mutex<std::time::Instant>>,\n}\n\n/// Serialized session info for list/detail endpoints.\n#[derive(Clone, serde::Serialize, serde::Deserialize, Debug)]\npub struct SessionInfo {\n    pub id: String,\n    pub created_at: String,\n    pub message_count: usize,\n    /// Optional human-readable title, set via `PATCH /sessions/:id`.\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    pub title: Option<String>,\n}\n\n/// Request body for `POST /sessions`.\n#[derive(serde::Deserialize, Debug)]\npub struct CreateSessionRequest {\n    pub system_prompt: Option<String>,\n    /// Append additional text to the server's default system prompt instead of\n    /// replacing it. Ignored when `system_prompt` is also provided.\n    pub append_system_prompt: Option<String>,\n    /// Human-readable display name for the session (shown in session list /\n    /// resume picker).\n    pub session_name: Option<String>,\n    /// Maximum number of steps (tool calls) allowed in this session.\n    pub max_steps: Option<u32>,\n    /// Extended-thinking token budget for models that support it (e.g.\n    /// Anthropic claude-3-7). `0` disables thinking.\n    pub thinking_budget: Option<u32>,\n    /// Permission mode: `\"default\"`, `\"auto\"`, `\"strict\"`, or `\"bypass\"`.\n    pub permission_mode: Option<String>,\n    /// Maximum total API spend in USD for this session. Agent stops after any\n    /// turn that would exceed this limit.\n    pub max_budget_usd: Option<f64>,\n}\n\n/// Response body for `POST /sessions`.\n#[derive(serde::Serialize, Debug)]\npub struct CreateSessionResponse {\n    pub id: String,\n    pub created_at: String,\n}\n\n/// Request body for `POST /sessions/:id/messages`.\n#[derive(serde::Deserialize, Debug)]\npub struct SessionMessageRequest {\n    pub content: String,\n}\n\n/// Response body for `POST /sessions/:id/messages`.\n#[derive(serde::Serialize, Debug)]\npub struct SessionMessageResponse {\n    pub role: String,\n    pub content: String,\n}\n\n/// Detail response for `GET /sessions/:id`.\n#[derive(serde::Serialize, Debug)]\npub struct SessionDetailResponse {\n    pub id: String,\n    pub created_at: String,\n    /// Optional human-readable title (set via `PATCH /sessions/:id`).\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    pub title: Option<String>,\n    pub messages: Vec<serde_json::Value>,\n    /// Goal-167: current task list as maintained by `todo_write` calls.\n    pub todos: Vec<crate::tools::todo::TodoItem>,\n    /// Current session lifecycle state: `\"idle\"` | `\"plan_pending_approval\"`.\n    pub status: String,\n    /// Non-null when `status` is `\"plan_pending_approval\"`.\n    pub pending_plan: Option<String>,\n    /// Goal-168: active goal state, or `null` when no goal is set.\n    pub goal: Option<crate::runtime::GoalState>,\n    /// First user message in the session (for quick display).\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    pub first_prompt: Option<String>,\n    /// Most recent user message in the session.\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    pub last_prompt: Option<String>,\n}\n\n// ── Goal-168: goal endpoint types ────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Request body for `POST /sessions/:id/goal`.\n#[derive(serde::Deserialize, Debug)]\npub struct SetGoalRequest {\n    /// The completion condition (free-form text).\n    pub condition: String,\n    /// Hard cap on autonomous turns. Defaults to 20.\n    pub max_turns: Option<u32>,\n}\n\n/// Response body for goal mutation endpoints.\n#[derive(serde::Serialize, Debug)]\npub struct GoalResponse {\n    pub status: String,\n}\n\n// ── Goal-169: slash commands endpoint types ───────────────────────────────\n\n/// One slash command entry in `GET /slash-commands`.\n#[derive(Clone, serde::Serialize, Debug)]\npub struct SlashCommandInfo {\n    pub name: String,\n    pub description: String,\n    pub source: String,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Vec::is_empty\")]\n    pub aliases: Vec<String>,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"String::is_empty\")]\n    pub argument_hint: String,\n}\n\n// ── SSE event types ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// A single block of message content (mirrors Claude Agent SDK's\n/// `TextBlock` / `ToolUseBlock`). Emitted as part of [`SseEvent::Message`]\n/// so SDK clients can iterate `for block in msg.content` without doing a\n/// second round-trip to the session detail endpoint.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, serde::Serialize, serde::Deserialize, PartialEq)]\n#[serde(tag = \"type\", rename_all = \"snake_case\")]\npub enum SseContentBlock {\n    /// A run of plain text from the assistant.\n    Text { text: String },\n    /// A request from the assistant to call a tool.\n    ToolUse {\n        id: String,\n        name: String,\n        input: serde_json::Value,\n    },\n}\n\n/// Server-Sent Event payload emitted during an agent session run.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, serde::Serialize, serde::Deserialize, PartialEq)]\n#[serde(tag = \"type\", rename_all = \"snake_case\")]\npub enum SseEvent {\n    /// A full role-tagged message, with content broken into typed blocks.\n    /// Modeled on Claude Agent SDK's `AssistantMessage` / `UserMessage`\n    /// streaming shape so the TS / Python SDKs can yield typed messages\n    /// without falling back to the session detail endpoint.\n    Message {\n        role: String,\n        content: Vec<SseContentBlock>,\n    },\n    /// A partial text delta during streaming. Concatenate `text` deltas\n    /// keyed by `step` to reconstruct the eventual `Message::Text` block.\n    PartialMessage { text: String, step: usize },\n    /// A tool is being called.\n    ToolCall { name: String, step: usize },\n    /// A tool call completed.\n    ToolResult { name: String, success: bool },\n    /// The agent run completed.\n    Done {\n        finish_reason: String,\n        total_steps: usize,\n    },\n    /// An error occurred.\n    Error { message: String },\n    /// Agent proposed a plan and is waiting for human review.\n    PlanProposed { plan: String },\n    /// Goal-168: judge found condition not yet met; loop continues.\n    GoalContinuing { reason: String, turns: u32 },\n    /// Goal-168: judge confirmed condition met.\n    GoalAchieved { condition: String, turns: u32 },\n    /// SDK Phase B: a tool call just completed; elapsed_ms is wall-clock time\n    /// from when the ToolCall event was received to when ToolResult arrived.\n    /// Emitted in addition to (and after) the `tool_result` event.\n    ToolProgress {\n        tool_use_id: String,\n        tool_name: String,\n        elapsed_ms: u64,\n    },\n}\n\n// ── App state ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Shared application state for the HTTP server.\n#[derive(Clone)]\npub struct AppState {\n    pub tools: Vec<ToolInfo>,\n    /// Live tool registry used to construct per-request and per-session\n    /// AgentRuntimes. Without this, runtimes get an empty registry and\n    /// every tool_call from the LLM resolves to \"tool not found\".\n    pub tool_registry: ToolRegistry,\n    pub config: Config,\n    pub provider: Arc<dyn LlmProvider>,\n    /// Session state keyed by session ID.\n    pub sessions: Arc<RwLock<HashMap<String, SessionState>>>,\n    /// Per-session SSE broadcast channels.\n    pub event_channels: Arc<RwLock<HashMap<String, broadcast::Sender<SseEvent>>>>,\n    pub metrics: Arc<Metrics>,\n    /// Goal-169: registered slash commands (built-in + skill-backed).\n    /// Pre-built at startup for cheap `GET /slash-commands` responses.\n    pub slash_commands: Arc<Vec<SlashCommandInfo>>,\n    pub session_ttl_secs: u64,\n    /// Semaphore limiting concurrent agent runs. Acquired in `run_agent` and\n    /// `send_session_message` before creating an `AgentRuntime`. When the\n    /// configured `max_concurrent_runs` is 0 (unlimited), this is initialised\n    /// with `Semaphore::MAX_PERMITS`.\n    pub run_semaphore: Arc<tokio::sync::Semaphore>,\n}\n\n/// Serializable tool info for the `/tools` endpoint.\n#[derive(Clone, serde::Serialize, serde::Deserialize, Debug)]\npub struct ToolInfo {\n    pub name: String,\n    pub description: String,\n    pub parameters: serde_json::Value,\n}\n\n/// Request body for `POST /run`.\n#[derive(serde::Deserialize, Debug)]\npub struct RunRequest {\n    pub goal: String,\n    pub max_steps: Option<u32>,\n    pub system_prompt: Option<String>,\n    /// Append additional text to the server's default system prompt instead of\n    /// replacing it. Ignored when `system_prompt` is also provided.\n    pub append_system_prompt: Option<String>,\n    /// Extended-thinking token budget for models that support it (e.g.\n    /// Anthropic claude-3-7). `0` disables thinking.\n    pub thinking_budget: Option<u32>,\n    /// Permission mode: `\"default\"`, `\"auto\"`, `\"strict\"`, or `\"bypass\"`.\n    pub permission_mode: Option<String>,\n    /// Maximum total API spend in USD for this run.\n    pub max_budget_usd: Option<f64>,\n}\n\n/// Successful response from `POST /run`.\n#[derive(serde::Serialize, Debug)]\npub struct RunResponse {\n    pub status: String,\n    pub finish_reason: String,\n    pub messages: Vec<serde_json::Value>,\n    pub usage: UsageInfo,\n}\n\n/// Token/step usage information.\n#[derive(serde::Serialize, Debug)]\npub struct UsageInfo {\n    pub total_steps: u32,\n    pub total_tokens: u64,\n}\n\n/// Error response body.\n#[derive(serde::Serialize, Debug)]\npub struct ErrorResponse {\n    pub status: String,\n    pub error: String,\n}\n\n/// Query parameters for `GET /sessions`.\n#[derive(serde::Deserialize, Debug, Default)]\npub struct ListSessionsQuery {\n    /// Maximum number of sessions to return (default: all).\n    pub limit: Option<usize>,\n    /// Number of sessions to skip before returning results (default: 0).\n    pub offset: Option<usize>,\n}\n\n// ── Router builders ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Build the axum [`Router`] with all API routes.\n///\n/// Routes:\n/// - `GET /health` — returns `\"ok\"` (200)\n/// - `GET /tools` — returns JSON array of [`ToolInfo`]\n/// - `POST /run` — runs the agent with a goal and returns the outcome\n/// - `POST /sessions` — create a new session\n/// - `GET /sessions` — list all sessions\n/// - `GET /sessions/:id` — get session detail with messages\n/// - `POST /sessions/:id/messages` — send a message in a session\n/// - `DELETE /sessions/:id` — remove a session\n/// - `GET /sessions/:id/events` — SSE stream of agent events for a session\n/// - `GET /openapi.json` — returns the OpenAPI 3.0.3 specification\n///\n/// Auth is sourced from the `RECURSIVE_HTTP_AUTH_KEYS` env var. For tests\n/// that need a deterministic auth state (no env-var races across parallel\n/// test threads), use [`build_router_with_auth`] instead.\npub fn build_router(state: AppState) -> Router {\n    build_router_with_auth(state, auth_config_from_env())\n}\n\n/// Build the HTTP router with an explicit `AuthConfig`.\n///\n/// Tests use this to inject a known auth state without touching\n/// process-global env vars. Production code paths use [`build_router`].\n///\n/// The rate limiter is sourced from env (`rate_limiter_from_env`).\n/// Tests that need deterministic rate-limit behavior should use\n/// [`build_router_with_auth_and_rate_limit`] instead.\npub fn build_router_with_auth(state: AppState, auth: AuthConfig) -> Router {\n    build_router_with_auth_and_rate_limit(state, auth, rate_limiter_from_env())\n}\n\n/// Build the HTTP router with an explicit `AuthConfig` AND an explicit\n/// `RateLimiter`.\n///\n/// This is the lowest-level constructor — both of the layered\n/// middleware states are caller-supplied. Production code paths\n/// invoke [`build_router`] (env-driven on both); tests that need\n/// race-free rate-limit assertions use this directly.\npub fn build_router_with_auth_and_rate_limit(\n    state: AppState,\n    auth: AuthConfig,\n    limiter: RateLimiter,\n) -> Router {\n    Router::new()\n        .route(\"/health\", get(health))\n        .route(\"/tools\", get(list_tools))\n        .route(\"/run\", post(run_agent))\n        .route(\"/sessions\", post(create_session))\n        .route(\"/sessions\", get(list_sessions))\n        .route(\"/sessions/{id}\", get(get_session))\n        .route(\"/sessions/{id}\", axum::routing::delete(delete_session))\n        .route(\"/sessions/{id}\", axum::routing::patch(patch_session))\n        .route(\"/sessions/{id}/messages\", post(send_session_message))\n        .route(\"/sessions/{id}/events\", get(session_events))\n        .route(\"/sessions/{id}/plan/confirm\", post(session_plan_confirm))\n        .route(\"/sessions/{id}/plan/reject\", post(session_plan_reject))\n        // Goal-168: goal loop endpoints.\n        .route(\"/sessions/{id}/goal\", post(session_set_goal))\n        .route(\n            \"/sessions/{id}/goal\",\n            axum::routing::delete(session_clear_goal),\n        )\n        // Goal-170: interrupt the current agent turn.\n        .route(\"/sessions/{id}/interrupt\", post(session_interrupt))\n        // SDK Phase C: fork a session.\n        .route(\"/sessions/{id}/fork\", post(fork_session))\n        // Goal-169: slash commands listing.\n        .route(\"/slash-commands\", get(list_slash_commands))\n        .route(\"/agui\", post(agui_run))\n        .route(\"/openapi.json\", get(openapi_spec))\n        .route(\"/metrics\", get(metrics_handler))\n        .layer(axum::middleware::from_fn_with_state(\n            state.metrics.clone(),\n            metrics_middleware,\n        ))\n        .layer(axum::middleware::from_fn_with_state(auth, auth_middleware))\n        // rate_limit is added last so it is the outermost layer and runs\n        // before auth — this ensures unauthenticated (brute-force) requests\n        // are counted against the IP-based bucket and cannot bypass limits by\n        // rotating API keys (SEC-006).\n        .layer(axum::middleware::from_fn_with_state(\n            limiter,\n            rate_limit_middleware,\n        ))\n        .layer(DefaultBodyLimit::max(MAX_BODY_BYTES))\n        .with_state(Arc::new(state))\n}\n\n/// Build a static OpenAPI 3.0.3 specification describing all API endpoints.\npub fn build_openapi_spec() -> serde_json::Value {\n    serde_json::json!({\n        \"openapi\": \"3.0.3\",\n        \"info\": {\n            \"title\": \"Recursive Agent API\",\n            \"version\": \"0.4.0\",\n            \"description\": \"HTTP API for the Recursive coding agent\"\n        },\n        \"paths\": {\n            \"/health\": {\n                \"get\": {\n                    \"summary\": \"Health check\",\n                    \"description\": \"Returns 'ok' if the server is running.\",\n                    \"responses\": {\n                        \"200\": {\n                            \"description\": \"Server is healthy\",\n                            \"content\": {\n                                \"text/plain\": {\n                                    \"schema\": { \"type\": \"string\", \"example\": \"ok\" }\n                                }\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            },\n            \"/tools\": {\n                \"get\": {\n                    \"summary\": \"List registered tools\",\n                    \"description\": \"Returns the JSON array of tools available to the agent.\",\n                    \"responses\": {\n                        \"200\": {\n                            \"description\": \"Array of tool descriptors\",\n                            \"content\": {\n                                \"application/json\": {\n                                    \"schema\": {\n                                        \"type\": \"array\",\n                                        \"items\": { \"$ref\": \"#/components/schemas/ToolInfo\" }\n                                    }\n                                }\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            },\n            \"/run\": {\n                \"post\": {\n                    \"summary\": \"Run the agent\",\n                    \"description\": \"Execute the agent with a goal and return the outcome.\",\n                    \"requestBody\": {\n                        \"required\": true,\n                        \"content\": {\n                            \"application/json\": {\n                                \"schema\": { \"$ref\": \"#/components/schemas/RunRequest\" }\n                            }\n                        }\n                    },\n                    \"responses\": {\n                        \"200\": {\n                            \"description\": \"Agent completed successfully\",\n                            \"content\": {\n                                \"application/json\": {\n                                    \"schema\": { \"$ref\": \"#/components/schemas/RunResponse\" }\n                                }\n                            }\n                        },\n                        \"400\": {\n                            \"description\": \"Invalid request (e.g. empty goal)\",\n                            \"content\": {\n                                \"application/json\": {\n                                    \"schema\": { \"$ref\": \"#/components/schemas/ErrorResponse\" }\n                                }\n                            }\n                        },\n                        \"422\": { \"description\": \"Request body failed deserialization\" },\n                        \"500\": {\n                            \"description\": \"Internal server error\",\n                            \"content\": {\n                                \"application/json\": {\n                                    \"schema\": { \"$ref\": \"#/components/schemas/ErrorResponse\" }\n                                }\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            },\n            \"/sessions\": {\n                \"get\": {\n                    \"summary\": \"List sessions\",\n                    \"description\": \"Returns all active sessions.\",\n                    \"responses\": {\n                        \"200\": {\n                            \"description\": \"Array of session info objects\",\n                            \"content\": {\n                                \"application/json\": {\n                                    \"schema\": {\n                                        \"type\": \"array\",\n                                        \"items\": { \"$ref\": \"#/components/schemas/SessionInfo\" }\n                                    }\n                                }\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                },\n                \"post\": {\n                    \"summary\": \"Create a session\",\n                    \"description\": \"Create a new multi-turn conversation session.\",\n                    \"requestBody\": {\n                        \"required\": true,\n                        \"content\": {\n                            \"application/json\": {\n                                \"schema\": { \"$ref\": \"#/components/schemas/CreateSessionRequest\" }\n                            }\n                        }\n                    },\n                    \"responses\": {\n                        \"201\": {\n                            \"description\": \"Session created\",\n                            \"content\": {\n                                \"application/json\": {\n                                    \"schema\": { \"$ref\": \"#/components/schemas/CreateSessionResponse\" }\n                                }\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            },\n            \"/sessions/{id}\": {\n                \"get\": {\n                    \"summary\": \"Get session detail\",\n                    \"description\": \"Returns session metadata and full message transcript.\",\n                    \"parameters\": [{\n                        \"name\": \"id\",\n                        \"in\": \"path\",\n                        \"required\": true,\n                        \"schema\": { \"type\": \"string\" }\n                    }],\n                    \"responses\": {\n                        \"200\": {\n                            \"description\": \"Session detail with messages\",\n                            \"content\": {\n                                \"application/json\": {\n                                    \"schema\": { \"$ref\": \"#/components/schemas/SessionDetailResponse\" }\n                                }\n                            }\n                        },\n                        \"404\": { \"description\": \"Session not found\" }\n                    }\n                },\n                \"delete\": {\n                    \"summary\": \"Delete a session\",\n                    \"description\": \"Remove a session and its transcript.\",\n                    \"parameters\": [{\n                        \"name\": \"id\",\n                        \"in\": \"path\",\n                        \"required\": true,\n                        \"schema\": { \"type\": \"string\" }\n                    }],\n                    \"responses\": {\n                        \"204\": { \"description\": \"Session deleted\" },\n                        \"404\": { \"description\": \"Session not found\" }\n                    }\n                }\n            },\n            \"/sessions/{id}/messages\": {\n                \"post\": {\n                    \"summary\": \"Send a message\",\n                    \"description\": \"Send a user message in a session and get the assistant response.\",\n                    \"parameters\": [{\n                        \"name\": \"id\",\n                        \"in\": \"path\",\n                        \"required\": true,\n                        \"schema\": { \"type\": \"string\" }\n                    }],\n                    \"requestBody\": {\n                        \"required\": true,\n                        \"content\": {\n                            \"application/json\": {\n                                \"schema\": { \"$ref\": \"#/components/schemas/SessionMessageRequest\" }\n                            }\n                        }\n                    },\n                    \"responses\": {\n                        \"200\": {\n                            \"description\": \"Assistant response\",\n                            \"content\": {\n                                \"application/json\": {\n                                    \"schema\": { \"$ref\": \"#/components/schemas/SessionMessageResponse\" }\n                                }\n                            }\n                        },\n                        \"404\": {\n                            \"description\": \"Session not found\",\n                            \"content\": {\n                                \"application/json\": {\n                                    \"schema\": { \"$ref\": \"#/components/schemas/ErrorResponse\" }\n                                }\n                            }\n                        },\n                        \"500\": {\n                            \"description\": \"Internal server error\",\n                            \"content\": {\n                                \"application/json\": {\n                                    \"schema\": { \"$ref\": \"#/components/schemas/ErrorResponse\" }\n                                }\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            },\n            \"/sessions/{id}/events\": {\n                \"get\": {\n                    \"summary\": \"Subscribe to session events\",\n                    \"description\": \"SSE stream of real-time agent events for a session.\",\n                    \"parameters\": [{\n                        \"name\": \"id\",\n                        \"in\": \"path\",\n                        \"required\": true,\n                        \"schema\": { \"type\": \"string\" }\n                    }],\n                    \"responses\": {\n                        \"200\": {\n                            \"description\": \"SSE event stream\",\n                            \"content\": {\n                                \"text/event-stream\": {\n                                    \"schema\": { \"type\": \"string\" }\n                                }\n                            }\n                        },\n                        \"404\": { \"description\": \"Session not found\" }\n                    }\n                }\n            },\n            \"/agui\": {\n                \"post\": {\n                    \"summary\": \"Run an AG-UI agent\",\n                    \"description\": \"Drive a recursive agent run via the AG-UI protocol \\\n                        (https://docs.ag-ui.com). Body is an AG-UI RunAgentInput; the \\\n                        response is an SSE stream of AG-UI events (RunStarted, \\\n                        TextMessageStart/Content/End, ToolCall*, RunFinished, ...).\",\n                    \"requestBody\": {\n                        \"required\": true,\n                        \"content\": {\n                            \"application/json\": {\n                                \"schema\": { \"type\": \"object\" },\n                                \"description\": \"AG-UI RunAgentInput payload\"\n                            }\n                        }\n                    },\n                    \"responses\": {\n                        \"200\": {\n                            \"description\": \"AG-UI SSE event stream\",\n                            \"content\": {\n                                \"text/event-stream\": {\n                                    \"schema\": { \"type\": \"string\" }\n                                }\n                            }\n                        },\n                        \"400\": { \"description\": \"Invalid AG-UI RunAgentInput\" }\n                    }\n                }\n            },\n            \"/openapi.json\": {\n                \"get\": {\n                    \"summary\": \"OpenAPI specification\",\n                    \"description\": \"Returns this OpenAPI 3.0.3 spec as JSON.\",\n                    \"responses\": {\n                        \"200\": {\n                            \"description\": \"OpenAPI spec document\",\n                            \"content\": {\n                                \"application/json\": {\n                                    \"schema\": { \"type\": \"object\" }\n                                }\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        },\n        \"components\": {\n            \"schemas\": {\n                \"ToolInfo\": {\n                    \"type\": \"object\",\n                    \"properties\": {\n                        \"name\": { \"type\": \"string\" },\n                        \"description\": { \"type\": \"string\" },\n                        \"parameters\": { \"type\": \"object\" }\n                    },\n                    \"required\": [\"name\", \"description\", \"parameters\"]\n                },\n                \"RunRequest\": {\n                    \"type\": \"object\",\n                    \"properties\": {\n                        \"goal\": { \"type\": \"string\" },\n                        \"max_steps\": { \"type\": \"integer\", \"nullable\": true },\n                        \"system_prompt\": { \"type\": \"string\", \"nullable\": true },\n                        \"append_system_prompt\": { \"type\": \"string\", \"nullable\": true },\n                        \"thinking_budget\": { \"type\": \"integer\", \"nullable\": true },\n                        \"permission_mode\": { \"type\": \"string\", \"enum\": [\"default\", \"auto\", \"strict\", \"bypass\"], \"nullable\": true },\n                        \"max_budget_usd\": { \"type\": \"number\", \"nullable\": true }\n                    },\n                    \"required\": [\"goal\"]\n                },\n                \"RunResponse\": {\n                    \"type\": \"object\",\n                    \"properties\": {\n                        \"status\": { \"type\": \"string\" },\n                        \"finish_reason\": { \"type\": \"string\" },\n                        \"messages\": { \"type\": \"array\", \"items\": { \"type\": \"object\" } },\n                        \"usage\": { \"$ref\": \"#/components/schemas/UsageInfo\" }\n                    },\n                    \"required\": [\"status\", \"finish_reason\", \"messages\", \"usage\"]\n                },\n                \"UsageInfo\": {\n                    \"type\": \"object\",\n                    \"properties\": {\n                        \"total_steps\": { \"type\": \"integer\" },\n                        \"total_tokens\": { \"type\": \"integer\" }\n                    },\n                    \"required\": [\"total_steps\", \"total_tokens\"]\n                },\n                \"ErrorResponse\": {\n                    \"type\": \"object\",\n                    \"properties\": {\n                        \"status\": { \"type\": \"string\" },\n                        \"error\": { \"type\": \"string\" }\n                    },\n                    \"required\": [\"status\", \"error\"]\n                },\n              \"max_steps\": { \"type\": \"integer\", \"nullable\": true },\n                        \"thinking_budget\": { \"type\": \"integer\", \"nullable\": true },\n                        \"permission_mode\": { \"type\": \"string\", \"enum\": [\"default\", \"auto\", \"strict\", \"bypass\"], \"nullable\": true },\n                        \"max_budget_usd\": { \"type\": \"number\", \"nullable\": true }\n                    }\n                },\n                \"CreateSessionResponse\": {\n                    \"type\": \"object\",\n                    \"properties\": {\n                        \"id\": { \"type\": \"string\" },\n                        \"created_at\": { \"type\": \"string\" }\n                    },\n                    \"required\": [\"id\", \"created_at\"]\n                },\n                \"SessionInfo\": {\n                    \"type\": \"object\",\n                    \"properties\": {\n                        \"id\": { \"type\": \"string\" },\n                        \"created_at\": { \"type\": \"string\" },\n                        \"message_count\": { \"type\": \"integer\" }\n                    },\n                    \"required\": [\"id\", \"created_at\", \"message_count\"]\n                },\n                \"SessionDetailResponse\": {\n                    \"type\": \"object\",\n                    \"properties\": {\n                        \"id\": { \"type\": \"string\" },\n                        \"created_at\": { \"type\": \"string\" },\n                        \"messages\": { \"type\": \"array\", \"items\": { \"type\": \"object\" } }\n                    },\n                    \"required\": [\"id\", \"created_at\", \"messages\"]\n                },\n                \"SessionMessageRequest\": {\n                    \"type\": \"object\",\n                    \"properties\": {\n                        \"content\": { \"type\": \"string\" }\n                    },\n                    \"required\": [\"content\"]\n                },\n                \"SessionMessageResponse\": {\n                    \"type\": \"object\",\n                    \"properties\": {\n                        \"role\": { \"type\": \"string\" },\n                        \"content\": { \"type\": \"string\" }\n                    },\n                    \"required\": [\"role\", \"content\"]\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    })\n}\n\n/// Spawn a background task that periodically evicts idle sessions.\n///\n/// Every `check_interval` seconds, the reaper scans all sessions and removes\n/// those whose `last_active` is older than `session_ttl_secs`. The reaper\n/// calls `runtime.close()` on each evicted session so the transcript is\n/// saved to the storage backend before the session is dropped.\npub fn spawn_session_reaper(\n    state: Arc<AppState>,\n    check_interval: std::time::Duration,\n) -> tokio::task::JoinHandle<()> {\n    tokio::spawn(async move {\n        loop {\n            tokio::time::sleep(check_interval).await;\n            let ttl = std::time::Duration::from_secs(state.session_ttl_secs);\n            let now = std::time::Instant::now();\n            let mut to_evict: Vec<String> = Vec::new();\n            // Phase 1: collect eviction candidates under a read lock.\n            {\n                let sessions = state.sessions.read().await;\n                for (id, session) in sessions.iter() {\n                    if now.saturating_duration_since(*session.last_active.lock().unwrap()) >= ttl {\n                        to_evict.push(id.clone());\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n            if to_evict.is_empty() {\n                continue;\n            }\n            // Phase 2: evict under a write lock, calling close() on each.\n            {\n                let mut sessions = state.sessions.write().await;\n                for id in &to_evict {\n                    if let Some(session) = sessions.remove(id) {\n                        // Try to close the runtime (best-effort — the lock\n                        // may be held by an in-flight turn).\n                        if let Ok(mut rt) = session.runtime.try_lock() {\n                            rt.close(None).await;\n                        }\n                        tracing::info!(\"reaper: evicted idle session {id}\");\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    })\n}\n","path":"src/http/mod.rs"}

state.config.system_prompt.clone();\n            if let Some(extra) = &body.append_system_prompt {\n                p.push('\\n');\n                p.push_str(extra);\n            }\n            p\n        }\n    };\n    let mut tool_registry = state.tool_registry.clone();\n    if let Some(mode_str) = body.permission_mode.as_deref() {\n        let perm_mode = parse_permission_mode(mode_str, state.config.allow_bypass_permissions);\n        tool_registry = tool_registry.with_permissions(LayeredPermissionsConfig {\n            mode: perm_mode,\n            layers: Vec::new(),\n        });\n    }\n\n    let mut runtime = AgentRuntimeBuilder::new()\n        .llm(state.provider.clone())\n        .tools(tool_registry)\n        .system_prompt(system_prompt)\n        .max_steps(max_steps)\n        .build()\n        .map_err(|e| {\n            (\n                StatusCode::INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,\n                Json(ErrorResponse {\n                    status: \"error\".into(),\n                    error: format!(\"failed to build runtime: {e}\"),\n                }),\n            )\n        })?;\n\n    let outcome = runtime.run(&body.goal).await.map_err(|e| {\n        record_run_failed(&state.metrics);\n        (\n            StatusCode::INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,\n            Json(ErrorResponse {\n                status: \"error\".into(),\n                error: format!(\"agent run failed: {e}\"),\n            }),\n        )\n    })?;\n\n    record_run_success(&state.metrics, outcome.steps, &outcome.total_usage);\n\n    // Serialize transcript messages to JSON values\n    let messages: Vec<serde_json::Value> = runtime\n        .transcript()\n        .iter()\n        .filter_map(|msg| serde_json::to_value(msg).ok())\n        .collect();\n\n    let finish_reason = outcome.finish_reason.to_string();\n\n    Ok(Json(RunResponse {\n        status: \"success\".into(),\n        finish_reason,\n        messages,\n        usage: UsageInfo {\n            total_steps: outcome.steps as u32,\n            total_tokens: outcome.total_usage.total_tokens as u64,\n        },\n    }))\n}\n\n// ── Request parsing helpers ────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Parse `permission_mode` string from an API request body.\n///\n/// Accepted values (case-insensitive): `\"default\"`, `\"auto\"`, `\"strict\"`,\n/// `\"bypass\"` / `\"bypass_permissions\"`. Unknown values fall back to `Default`.\nfn parse_permission_mode(s: &str, allow_bypass: bool) -> PermissionMode {\n    match s.to_ascii_lowercase().as_str() {\n        \"auto\" => PermissionMode::Auto,\n        \"strict\" => PermissionMode::Strict,\n        \"bypass\" | \"bypass_permissions\" if allow_bypass => PermissionMode::BypassPermissions,\n        _ => PermissionMode::Default,\n    }\n}\n\n// ── Session endpoints ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Generate a session ID using UUID v7 (time-ordered, globally unique).\nfn generate_session_id() -> String {\n    uuid::Uuid::now_v7().to_string()\n}\n\n/// Format a SystemTime as a basic ISO-8601 string (without chrono).\nfn format_timestamp(t: SystemTime) -> String {\n    let dur = t.duration_since(SystemTime::UNIX_EPOCH).unwrap_or_default();\n    let secs = dur.as_secs();\n    // Basic formatting: seconds since epoch as a simple numeric timestamp\n    // For a more human-readable format we do manual UTC conversion\n    let days = secs / 86400;\n    let remaining = secs % 86400;\n    let hours = remaining / 3600;\n    let minutes = (remaining % 3600) / 60;\n    let seconds = remaining % 60;\n\n    // Days since 1970-01-01 — delegate to the O(1) civil-calendar impl in session.rs\n","path":"src/http/handlers.rs"}

fn state(workspace: PathBuf, provider: Arc<MockProvider>) -> AppState {
    AppState {
        tools: vec![],
        config: mock_config(workspace),
        tool_registry: ToolRegistry::local(),
        provider,
        sessions: Arc::new(RwLock::new(HashMap::new())),
        event_channels: Arc::new(RwLock::new(HashMap::new())),
        metrics: Arc::new(Metrics::default()),
        slash_commands: Arc::new(Vec::new()),
        session_ttl_secs: 0,
            run_semaphore: std::sync::Arc::new(tokio::sync::Semaphore::new(8)),
    }
}

len(line.lstrip())]\n                                break\n                        if field_indent is None:\n                            field_indent = '            '  # default 12 spaces\n                        \n                        insertion = f\"\\n{field_indent}{field_line}\"\n                        content = content[:i] + insertion + content[i:]\n                    break\n                brace_count -= 1\n            i += 1\n    \n    with open(filepath, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(content)\n    print(f\"Updated {filepath}\")\n\n# Fix each file\nadd_field_to_config_struct('src/multi.rs', 'max_concurrent_runs: 8,')\nadd_field_to_config_struct('src/tools/team_manage.rs', 'max_concurrent_runs: 8,')\nadd_field_to_config_struct('src/main.rs', 'max_concurrent_runs: 8,')\nadd_field_to_config_struct('tests/agui_e2e.rs', 'max_concurrent_runs: 8,')\nadd_field_to_config_struct('tests/agent_team_integration.rs', 'max_concurrent_runs: 8,')\nPYEOF\n"}

## Summary of Changes

### Core Implementation

1. **`src/config.rs`** — Added `max_concurrent_runs: usize` field to `Config` struct with default value `8`, read from `RECURSIVE_MAX_CONCURRENT_RUNS` env var.

2. **`src/http/mod.rs`** — Added `run_semaphore: Arc<Semaphore>` field to `AppState` struct.

3. **`src/http/handlers.rs`** — In the `run_handler`, acquire a semaphore permit before processing a run request. If the semaphore is exhausted, return `503 SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE` with a descriptive error message. The permit is held for the duration of the run, limiting concurrent runs.

### Wiring in main.rs

4. **`src/main.rs`** — In the HTTP server setup, read `config.max_concurrent_runs`, create a `Semaphore` with that many permits (or `MAX_PERMITS` if 0, minimum 1), and pass it as `run_semaphore` to `AppState`.

### Test Fixes

5. **`tests/http.rs`** — Added `max_concurrent_runs: 8` to all `Config {` initializers and `run_semaphore` to all `AppState {` initializers (10 occurrences each).

6. **`tests/v050_integration.rs`** — Added `max_concurrent_runs: 8` to `Config` initializer and `run_semaphore` to `AppState` initializer.

7. **`tests/agui_e2e.rs`** — Added `max_concurrent_runs: 8` to `Config` initializer and `run_semaphore` to `AppState` initializer.

8. **`tests/agent_team_integration.rs`** — Added `max_concurrent_runs: 8` to `Config` initializer.

9. **`src/multi.rs`** — Added `max_concurrent_runs: 8` to `Config` initializer in test.

10. **`src/tools/team_manage.rs`** — Added `max_concurrent_runs: 8` to `Config` initializer in test.
